        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1300302156" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7313808548742454914"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431890566i/14878986.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437292364i/15565742.jpg' width='100"/' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>Title:</b> Tyrant<br/><b>Series:</b> King, #2<br/><b>Author:</b> T.M. Frazier<br/><b>Release date: </b> 16th August, 2015<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br/><b> HEA: </b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ Yes  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396707796i/9175086.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439491786i/15844865._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>First things first, a massive round of applause to you T.M. Frazier! You really pulled it out the bag with Tyrant. I'll freely admit, whilst I enjoyed King, I wasn't completely sold as much as I would have hoped. This time around, I was sucked right in. It had the added barrage of action, tension and adrenaline I craved in the first book in the series, with </span>
  <span id="freeText7313808548742454914" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431890566i/14878986.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437292364i/15565742.jpg" width='100"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Title:</b> Tyrant<br><b>Series:</b> King, #2<br><b>Author:</b> T.M. Frazier<br><b>Release date: </b> 16th August, 2015<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br><b> HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396707796i/9175086.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439491786i/15844865._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>First things first, a massive round of applause to you T.M. Frazier! You really pulled it out the bag with Tyrant. I'll freely admit, whilst I enjoyed King, I wasn't completely sold as much as I would have hoped. This time around, I was sucked right in. It had the added barrage of action, tension and adrenaline I craved in the first book in the series, with the unique blend of romance and intimacy I've come to recognise in Doe and King's relationship.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439751073ra/15880280.gif" width="200" height="100" alt=" photo D4651015-218D-481B-8E8E-656A07031CE6_zpscah7pt4a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439751074ra/15880281.gif" height="100" width="200" alt=" photo 70D3D2DA-3551-429A-8834-E8CAE0BF04DE_zpswp8kb90x.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Tyrant begins in the direct aftermath of the explosive revelations made in King and like Doe, we are trying to navigate through what is real and who can be trusted. They were plenty of light bulb moments reading this and even as pieces of the puzzle were beginning to fall in place, the author added new exciting elements to the story.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439751074ra/15880282.gif" width="200" height='100"' alt=" photo 6584819C-CBBF-445E-BFC3-AF011AE4A013_zpsyptxi8jp.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439755022ra/15881013.gif" width="200" alt=" photo 4BAD4494-5027-417C-8D3B-D764DAE9BD4B_zps1e37vv68.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I didn't expect to love it as much as I did and I also didn't expect the amount of emotion that this book evoked. Sadness, anguish, revulsion, anger but also heartwarming hilarious moments that are so unique to couple such as Doe and King. They had such remarkable strength; in themselves, in each other and in their bond which undoubtedly got them through.<br><br>I'm all aboard the King train and its full steam ahead for Bear's story. <span id="freeTextContainer15604065305523503753">I'm writing one review for this book "duo". Mainly for myself, so I can remember why the lower rating. I enjoyed the story...however, the execution was awkward, the plot was riddled with glaring and uncomfortable holes <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ The heroine is stabbed twice in the leg...to the bone, but the wound is never mentioned again, she is raped but has no aftereffects and goes on to have sex within days  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, and the violence was extreme. Rape of important people <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ the hero</span></span>
  <span id="freeText15604065305523503753" style="display:none">I'm writing one review for this book "duo". Mainly for myself, so I can remember why the lower rating. I enjoyed the story...however, the execution was awkward, the plot was riddled with glaring and uncomfortable holes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The heroine is stabbed twice in the leg...to the bone, but the wound is never mentioned again, she is raped but has no aftereffects and goes on to have sex within days  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, and the violence was extreme. Rape of important people <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ the heroine is raped, King's childhood friend is raped in a flashback, and another of King's friends is raped by a gang with a stick of some sort  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> constant blood and gore, the death of many likeable characters, and King's over the top high-handed bossiness wore me the eff out. Each book was around 200 pages, the first of which ends on a major cliffhanger. I think this could have either been pared down into one book with less drama or lengthened and strengthened by some hard core beta reads and editing. As is, it felt thrown out there and unfinished. It was a good bare bones plot, and I think I'm more bummed at the lost potential than anything else. </span>

<div id="review_1300323908" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1300323908" />
    <a title="Jasmine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine"><img alt="Jasmine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406624675p2/31339793.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1300323908?book_show_action=true">Jun 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasmine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasmine" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine">Jasmine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/25565707-tyrant">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=give-me-that-alpha-male">give-me-that-alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=panty-soaking-wet">panty-soaking-wet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=there-be-crazy-mofos">there-be-crazy-mofos</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=i-love-me-some-angst-drama">i-love-me-some-angst-drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=mind-fuck">mind-fuck</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=dark-deadly-dangerous">dark-deadly-dangerous</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=dying-in-agony-of-wait">dying-in-agony-of-wait</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=release-aug-2015">release-aug-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=dat-be-some-badass-motha-fucka">dat-be-some-badass-motha-fucka</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1300323908" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6311126920730385856"><b>4 STARS! ★★★★</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439728187i/15877395.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"I sometimes wish I could just forget it all, but I can't. I won't. Because I don't want to ever want to forget you. And I welcome this pain because it reminds me that you were real."</i>
</b><br/><br/>After finishing King back then with my jaw dropped open, needless to say that I've been waiting anxiously for Tyrant to be out. I went in mentally prepared thinking that I'll be getting the answers I'm looking for and while I did, the shocking twist in this epic conclusion completely stumped me! Wel</span>
  <span id="freeText6311126920730385856" style="display:none"><b>4 STARS! ★★★★</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439728187i/15877395.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"I sometimes wish I could just forget it all, but I can't. I won't. Because I don't want to ever want to forget you. And I welcome this pain because it reminds me that you were real."</i>
</b><br><br>After finishing King back then with my jaw dropped open, needless to say that I've been waiting anxiously for Tyrant to be out. I went in mentally prepared thinking that I'll be getting the answers I'm looking for and while I did, the shocking twist in this epic conclusion completely stumped me! Well played, T.M. Frazier. You really got me there.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435r/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Tyrant</u>
</b> picks up right after that one helluva cliffhanger in <b>
  <u>King</u>
</b> and without giving away too much, both King and Doe are left to deal with the aftermath of events. On one hand, we watch King plotting his revenge after having his loved ones snatched away from him. The other being Doe still coming to terms with the new revelations being thrown at her about her original past. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439734198i/15877863.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I'll admit, I was little worried there with how the author was gonna tie up some of these plot devices she threw in and my initial thought was "Oh boy this is not gonna end well." With the past catching up to the present, I was nervous with how Doe will choose one life over another. Will she stay with King once she remembered her entire past? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439734198i/15877862.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>While Doe is elsewhere dealing with her issues, King was just all sorts of badassery. Whenever we get a glimpse of his POV, it was non-stop intense. Together with Bear, they're both out for blood and the pages were just filled with suspense and action that had me worrying for their lives. <br><br>But absolutely nothing could prepare me for one mindblowing of a twist that I never saw coming from a mile away. It's just one of those moments when you try to process what just <i>really</i> happened and you go somewhere between "NO WAY" and "THAT IS GENIUS". Honestly, the way the author crafted the entire story from start to finish undoubtedly blew me away. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435r/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall Tyrant delivered the well-deserved conclusion to King and Doe's story and I believe readers who have been anxiously waiting for this will not be disappointed. The series had angst, suspense, steam, passionate love and even some good ole' humor; all wrapped up in one amazing package. After shedding some tears in the first one, I still found myself tearing up in this instalment (Because...pancakes &lt;- those who read the series will understand what I mean). <br><br>Now I'm really excited for some Bear in the future. So excited when the author announced we'll get his story towards the end of the year, fingers crossed!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i><u>Tyrant</u> is the conclusion to King &amp; Doe's story in the King series. It must be read after King.</i><br><br><b>
  <i>ARC kindly provided by the author in exchange for an honest review.</i>
</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433775460i/15140880.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="http://readescapadereviews.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275361.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.facebook.com/readingescapadeblog" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275362.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275363.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1365559962" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1365559962" />
    <a title="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3161105-maida---v--"><img alt="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1555353893p2/3161105.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1365559962?book_show_action=true">Aug 16, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" href="/user/show/3161105-maida---v--">Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=alpha-male-sexiness">alpha-male-sexiness</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=dark-reads">dark-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=delicious-men">delicious-men</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=books-of-2015">books-of-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=fave-books-of-2015">fave-books-of-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1365559962" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18234866283874648696"><br/><b>RATING: 4 “...a forever kind of thing” Hearts!! :)</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457842419i/18412546.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I sometimes wish I could just forget it all, but I can't. I won't. Because I don't want to ever want to forget you. And I welcome this pain because it reminds me that you were real."<br/></i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><i>Tyrant</i> is a dark and twisted sequel, one that captures the curtained brutality of our world with a starkly realistic and gritty expertise, and one featuring two charmingly flawed characters who, with their love story, bring a smile to our faces when the da</span>
  <span id="freeText18234866283874648696" style="display:none"><br><b>RATING: 4 “...a forever kind of thing” Hearts!! :)</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457842419i/18412546.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I sometimes wish I could just forget it all, but I can't. I won't. Because I don't want to ever want to forget you. And I welcome this pain because it reminds me that you were real."<br></i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><i>Tyrant</i> is a dark and twisted sequel, one that captures the curtained brutality of our world with a starkly realistic and gritty expertise, and one featuring two charmingly flawed characters who, with their love story, bring a smile to our faces when the darkness becomes overwhelming.<br><br>King is the perfect anti-hero, a tattooed badass with an unapologetic attitude and a delightfully foul mouth. Though he is a ruthless criminal of which he has no qualms about, his loyalty and protecting those he loves with unhinged determination are the qualities that make him so endearing. Unlike before when he made frustrating decisions we wish he wouldn’t, the way in which King is written in this gives him a transparent vulnerability, that softness to his edge making him feel delicately human. He’s a beautiful dichotomy of impressive faults and heartening strengths, and certainly holds his own as a memorable hero.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You seem to have forgotten who the fuck I am, Pup. So I'm going to remind you....<br>I'm the man who took you against your will and handcuffed you to my fucking bed. I'm the man who wanted you, so I fucking kept you. Do you really think you have a choice when it comes to being mine?"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>In addition to the mystery surrounding Doe’s lost memories, the revelation of her true identity and the appearance of her family, there’s also further romantic development between King and Doe. Amongst a past boyfriend she doesn’t remember and feeling betrayed by King, Doe is unsure of her standing with either man. Despite her confused and hurt feelings, she is still the admirable heroine we grew to love, upholding her backbone when it comes time to confront both her family and King. While she’s no doormat to King, she realizes her heart is King’s alone and their relationship is one full of the type of tension and pain that can only come from a couple who has established a visceral bond, leaving no doubts in our hearts and minds they will stand the test of time. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457842419i/18412547.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“In this world, there is very little I believe in, Pup. But I believe we belong together."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Overall <i>Tyrant</i> will likely not be a story for everyone, the dark theme uncompromising in its approach and Ms. Frazier refusing to shield readers from the rawness of the pain felt and the brutal but gratifying play out of events, yet there’s something undeniably spellbinding about the savagery of this world and its beautifully damaged inhabitants that keeps us coming back for more.<br><br><br><br><b>
  <i>Posted: March 12, 2016</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="18234866283874648696" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>

</a>

    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!

    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('IATUbXwPYJXFApYkXHV9bY5DPGOmmxRXiCg1H3dupHN/UO8cPhrjl25kHoVi82quDeakbacGwyf2XDoiH2Dp5Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('bxxTsDYiFilJbJFNAWXVffdpVYLq9i9cC0jtsiSXc8gwSGjBdDeVK+IKGew/48K+dMzNjOtr+Cx1POKPTJk+Xg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer5135708901822087370">T.M. (Tracey Marie) Frazier never dreamed that a single person would ever read a word she wrote when she published her first book. Now, she is a five-time USA Today bestselling author and her books have been translated into numerous languages and published all around the world. <br/><br/>T.M. enjoys writing what she calls ‘wrong side of the tracks romance’ with morally corrupt anti-heroes and ballsy heroine</span>
  <span id="freeText5135708901822087370" style="display:none">T.M. (Tracey Marie) Frazier never dreamed that a single person would ever read a word she wrote when she published her first book. Now, she is a five-time USA Today bestselling author and her books have been translated into numerous languages and published all around the world. <br /><br />T.M. enjoys writing what she calls ‘wrong side of the tracks romance’ with morally corrupt anti-heroes and ballsy heroines. <br /><br />Her books have been described as raw, dark and gritty. Basically, what that means, is while some authors are great at describing a flower as it blooms, T.M. is better at describing it in the final stages of decay. <br /><br />She loves meeting her readers, but if you see her at an event please don’t pinch her because she's not ready to wake up from this amazing dream. <br /><br />Join T.M. in Frazierland! <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/groups/tmfrazierland">www.facebook.com/groups/tmfrazierland</a></span>
